<user_id>102431877588231576041</user_id>< review>
FYI: Don't let them confuse you when considering a Moto Z Droid phone since the Motorola phones on display don't have tags indicating price or model. There are three models: Moto Play, Moto Z, and Moto Z Force (from least to most expensive).

Even with the display model briefly advertising which model it was while in "demo mode", the employee helping me incorrectly identified it and brushed off the video presentation as incorrect (but I knew better since I had done research).

Other sales associates will also probably try to get you to buy the more expensive "Force" model by suggesting it has the best battery of the three, but in reality the "Play" model  has the best battery (least expensive too), followed by the "Force" (shatterproof but expensive and not scratch resistant), and lastly the regular model (thinnest and not recommended).

Lastly, The Motorola Droid Turbo 2 is last year's shatterproof model (also not scratch resistant).

Do a little bit of research or you will be deceived on phones and plans!<//review>

< text>
We had family come up from L.A. and doing the escape rooms at the Code Zone in Petaluma were perfect for some great family bonding. The wonderful family who run the place were very nice and patient in accommodating our group of 14. We split into 2 groups, 1 group of adults and the other group made up of the kids. Code Zone was able to run both themed rooms concurrently so both of our groups could perform the rooms in the same 1 hour block.

Our plan was for the adults to do "X Marks The Spot" and the kids to do "Get To The Game." Both of our groups were able to beat our rooms and had so much fun doing so, we decided to book the next hour so we could swap rooms! Again, the adults were able to finish our room, while the kids came really close to finishing theirs. Super fun!

Completing the rooms was accomplished by dividing up tasks, with communication being the absolute key! If you see something, say something, because someone in your group may have come across something that may have you stumped. Overall, the rooms were really fun with the degree of difficulty of each being pretty comparable to one another.

I definitely would recommend Code Zone for a family group event or any other group setting for that matter, whether it be for a work team building excercise or just a group of friends getting together looking for some good fun! Thanks Code Zone! We had a blast!</text>

On Dec 31, 2019, I brought in an old Samsung Galaxy Tab S2 tablet, to replace the battery. They cut a tiny wire when they removed the back cover, and so had to order a new non-OEM battery AND a new OEM wire. After that the tablet would just go dead (something it never did before) in the middle of using it. The only way to revive it was to plug it in. In addition to that, the on-screen touch buttons were less responsive than they used to be (however, they later told me they were working normally despite my objections based on experience). I had to show them how the tablet was not functioning, and they sent it to an advanced repair center. They concluded the problem was just a defective battery, so they put a new battery in it and returned it to me. A few days later it died again. I brought it to them, and after a few hours they decided that they were done with it, called me to come get it, refunded me my money (sans sales tax), and told me they could do nothing more. That was yesterday, Jan 28, 2020. My tablet is now unable to consistently stay on for more than a few minutes without being constantly plugged in, which pretty much makes the new battery kind of pointless (also the battery they left in slowly drains even when plugged in). The on-screen touch buttons are now very unresponsive. I will probably have to buy a new tablet if I want to be mobile with it. This business with them was only supposed to take 2 days. Almost a month later, I wish I had never brought it to them. They were polite and refunded me most of the money that I paid to replace the battery, but they reimbursed me nothing to replace the tablet that they damaged, and they gave up on solving the problem that they caused. I will likely never go to them for this type of service again, and I will likely buy batteries/bulbs elsewhere.<//Review>

UPDATE!  The Koi Buffet is now open again! It's all the same great food as before. I just can't see the negative reviews here, cause service is great and the place is clean. The food is all fresh if you get here at a reasonable time. Best time is when they open! Fresh food and nobody has picked over all the food yet!  I gotta go back for those wings and ribs!

Closed for now due to the virus thing, but I really can't wait till it opens again! This is the best buffet in the area for a reasonable price. <user>113894885405412351787</user>< Text>
Pretty happy decision to eat there. Looked at the food before deciding and about 8/10 things looked pretty fresh. This was on a Thursday evening so maybe not the most busy time. At least not very busy when we were there. I imagine weekends to be busier.

This place is pretty big. Could seat many people if needed. Food was good and I think it's cool they have soft serve and regular ice cream.

Mostly pretty typical Asian buffet stuff with a few surprises. The Mei Fun was nice! Thin little rice noodles with a simple and warm flavor.

I might come back if I'm in the area and looking for a buffet again. Sushi wasn't great here but most non sushi buffets that offer it generally meet a low expectation for that.

Solid 4 stars. Service was friendly too! Maybe even more so than most buffets. I'll give them credit there.

5 stars if the sushi were better and more of the food items were fresh. But the price is quite good for what you're getting.

Maybe it's tough for buffets to compete at this price range though because Thunder Valley does a buffet that is bigger and about the same price for dinner on weekdays. Between the two, I'd have to give it to thunder but for the sake of variety I'd probably come here from time to time if I frequented this area a lot more.</Text>

<review>I am not sure why the others are saying the food isn't fresh and delicious.  It is every visit for me.  It must be the day and time of day I usually go (Sunday, about 1pm).  Everything is fresh and hot.  They couldn't restock crabs ü¶Ä fast enough. I enjoyed just about everything I normally would order at Chinese restaurants. I don't get food poisoning from eating there.

Three things I don't care for there: salad bar, sushi, and the grill to order meat. 1) Chinese food isn't about salad, it's about cook veggies. Don't eat that raw greens at buffet. 2) sushi is Japanese food. Chinese are notoriously bad at making sushi. If you ever had bad sushi, chances are the owner of that place is Chinese or Vietnamese.  3) I watch those guys grill...not sure what it is but they manage to burn the meat all the time. Plus they don't change tongs between raw and cooked meat. That's just asking for trouble. Avoid these 3 and you'll have a more enjoyable experience.

I dock a star for crappy service, as it is expected of Asian restaurants to have crappy service.< /review>< pictures>

<Time>1442261437767< /Time>< Review>
The service was wonderful, the people were very friendly, and were definitely on top of things. As for the food, it's mostly seafood oriented, so if you can't eat seafood or don't generally enjoy it, the number of items is severely limited. If you are a seafood buff, it looks very appetizing and I was very excited to see whole cooked crawfish among their selections, not something you generally see west of the Mississippi. I was also happy to see the bean-paste filled items, something my family greatly enjoys when we go to any oriental themed restaurant.
The soft serve ice cream, though, was definitely refreshing, having a vanilla custard flavor that was very delicious as opposed to the run-of-the-mill watered down vanilla you can find standard in a lot of other oriental buffets.
I would've been a lot happier, though, if there had been more beef-based products, or dishes that didn't have fattier-ended meats. The General Tso's chicken is also VERY Americanized, very sweet with very little spicy and sour. My current take-out place wins over The Golden Koi.</Review>
